 169: ```
 170: 
 171: Render whatever HTML/CSS/JS suits your domain. The WebView is isolated; only `platform.*` APIs cross the boundary.
 172: 
 173: **V1 card-render bridge:**
 174: - `platform.network.fetch(url, init)` ג€” works, gated by `declaredEndpoints` glob match
 175: - `platform.showNotification`, `platform.storage`, `platform.camera`, `platform.gallery`, `platform.file`, `platform.location`, `platform.message.respond` ג€” *reject* with a clear error in V1 inbox mode. For V1 dogfood, stick to `network.fetch`.
 176: 
 177: ## 4. Build + sign the plugin
 178: 
 179: ```sh
 180: # Install the SDK
 181: cd my-plugin
 182: npm install @syncler/plugin-sdk
 183: 
 184: # Build ג€” IIFE format, NOT ESM. The host loads the bundle inside a regular
 185: # `<script>` tag, which can't parse `export` statements.
 186: npx esbuild src/plugin.ts \
 187:   --bundle \
 188:   --format=iife \
 189:   --global-name=SynclerPluginExports \
 190:   --platform=browser \
 191:   --outfile=dist/plugin.bundle.js
 192: 
 193: # Sign it (positional args, tsx is required for the TS tool):
 194: npx tsx node_modules/@syncler/plugin-sdk/tools/sign-bundle.ts \
 195:   dist/plugin.bundle.js \
 196:   ~/.syncler/keys/sender.pem \
 197:   manifest.json \
 198:   manifest.signed.json
 199: ```
 200: 
 201: The tool signs the canonical-manifest-with-bundleHash-bytes (the exact bytes the Android host verifies against ג€” see `docs/crypto-spec.md` ֲ§5). `manifest.signed.json` will contain populated `bundleHash` + `signature` fields.
 202: 
 203: Host the bundle file at a stable HTTPS URL (CDN, S3, GitHub raw). For local development, debug builds of the Android app also accept plain `http://` URLs (e.g. a Python `-m http.server` on your LAN). Release builds require HTTPS.
 204: 
 205: ## 5. Publishing the plugin (your backend, one time per version)
 206: 
 207: ```python
 208: from syncler import Client
 209: import hashlib, json
 210: 
 211: client = Client(
 212:     sender_name="My App",
 213:     private_key_path="~/.syncler/keys/sender.pem",
 214:     base_url="https://api.syncler.app",
 215: )
 216: client.set_sender_id("<the sender_id Syncler issued you>")
 217: 
 218: bundle = open("dist/plugin.bundle.js", "rb").read()
 219: manifest = json.loads(open("manifest.signed.json").read())
 220: 
 221: response = client.publish_plugin(
 222:     plugin_identifier="com.example.myapp",
 223:     version="1.0.0",
 224:     manifest_hash=hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(
 225:         {k: v for k, v in manifest.items() if k != "signature"},
 226:         sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":")
 227:     ).encode()).digest(),
 228:     bundle_hash=hashlib.sha256(bundle).digest(),
 229:     bundle_signature=bytes.fromhex(manifest["signature"]),
 230:     signed_bundle_url="https://your-app.example.com/syncler-plugin.bundle.js",
 231:     renderer="script",
 232:     template=None,
 233:     card_type="event",
 234:     card_key_path=None,
 235:     capabilities=["network"],
 236:     endpoints=["https://your-app.example.com/api/*"],
 237: )
 238: 
 239: print("Published row:", response["plugin_row_id"])
 240: # Save this ג€” you'll need it in `send_to(plugin_id=...)`.
 241: 
 242: ### 5.1 Native Template Renderer
 243: 
 244: Set `renderer="template"` to ship a Compose-rendered native card instead of a JS bundle. The publish call looks like this:
 245: 
 246: ```python
 247: response = client.publish_plugin(
 248:     plugin_identifier="com.example.weather",
 249:     version="1.0.0",
 250:     manifest_hash=hashlib.sha256(b"manifest-placeholder").digest(),
 251:     bundle_hash=hashlib.sha256(b"unused-for-template").digest(),
 252:     bundle_signature=b"\x00" * 64,            # ignored for template
 253:     signed_bundle_url="https://example.com/unused",  # ignored for template
 254:     capabilities=[],
 255:     endpoints=["https://example.com/api/*"],
 256:     renderer="template",
 257:     template={
 258:         "layout": "standard_card",
 259:         "fields": {
 260:             "title":    {"path": "$.title"},
 261:             "subtitle": {"path": "$.subtitle"},
 262:             "body":     {"path": "$.body"},
 263:         },
 264:         "actions": [
 265:             {"id": "ack", "label": "Acknowledge", "endpoint": "https://example.com/api/ack"},
 266:         ],
 267:     },
 268: )
 269: ```
 270: 
 271: **JSONPath dialect.** Only `$.field(.subfield)*` is accepted. No array indexing (`$.items[0]`), no wildcards (`$.*`), no filters (`$.items[?(@.x>0)]`). Field-name segments must match `[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*`. The server rejects manifests with malformed paths at publish time, and the client-side resolver returns `null` for malformed input as a defense-in-depth.
 272: 
 273: **Layouts.** V1 ships one layout:
 274: 
 275: | Layout | Required fields | Optional fields | Notes |
 276: |---|---|---|---|
 277: | `standard_card` | `title` | `subtitle`, `body` | All values rendered as plain text via Compose `Text`. No markdown / HTML / link interpretation ג€” a hostile payload value cannot inject a clickable link. |
 278: 
 279: Additional layouts (`compact_row`, `score_card`, etc.) are deferred to a future phase.
 280: 
 281: **Actions.** Each action is a button on the card. When tapped, the host POSTs the **full decrypted payload as `application/json`** to `endpoint`. No `Authorization` header is attached ג€” the host explicitly uses an unauthenticated HTTP client for action POSTs so the user's Syncler bearer token never reaches your plugin endpoint (security boundary). If you need request authentication, HMAC the body using a sender-specific secret your backend knows out of band, or rely on TLS + endpoint allowlisting alone.
 282: 
 283: **Validation rules** the publish endpoint enforces (returns 422 otherwise):
 284: 
 285: - `layout` is in the supported set.
 286: - Required fields for the layout are present.
 287: - No fields outside the layout's allowed set.
 288: - Every `path` matches the JSONPath regex.
 289: - Every `action.endpoint` matches at least one of your declared `endpoints` globs (the same glob syntax that gates `platform.network.fetch` in script renderers).
 290: - Every `action.id` is unique within the template.
 291: 
 292: ### 5.2 Live Cards
 293: 
 294: Set `card_type="live"` to ship a persistent, upsertable card. The plugin manifest must also provide `card_key_path` ג€” a JSONPath into your decrypted payload that yields the stable identity for each card (e.g. `$.order_id`). This lets the inbox merge multiple upserts for the same logical card into one row.
 295: 
 296: ```python
 297: response = client.publish_plugin(
 298:     plugin_identifier="com.example.delivery",
 299:     version="1.0.0",
 300:     manifest_hash=hashlib.sha256(b"manifest").digest(),
 301:     bundle_hash=hashlib.sha256(open("dist/plugin.bundle.js","rb").read()).digest(),
 302:     bundle_signature=bytes.fromhex(manifest["signature"]),
 303:     signed_bundle_url="https://example.com/plugin.bundle.js",
 304:     capabilities=["network"],
 305:     endpoints=["https://example.com/api/*"],
 306:     card_type="live",
 307:     card_key_path="$.order_id",
 308: )
 309: ```
 310: 
 311: Live cards work with **either** renderer. The most common combo is `renderer="template"` + `card_type="live"` (delivery progress card with no JS).
 312: 
 313: #### Upserting a live card
 314: 
 315: ```python
 316: from syncler.crypto import assemble_live_card_aad, encrypt_payload
 317: from datetime import datetime, timedelta, UTC
 318: import json
 319: 
 320: expires_at = datetime.now(UTC) + timedelta(hours=12)
 321: 
 322: # Live card plaintext. Include `hostPreview` so the inbox row uses your
 323: # title/subtitle instead of the generic "New message from {sender_name}"
 324: # fallback. The `order_id` field is what the manifest's
 325: # `card_key_path="$.order_id"` resolves to and MUST equal the `card_key`
 326: # you pass to `upsert_card` below ג€” see the note after the example.
 327: plaintext = json.dumps({
 328:     "hostPreview": {
 329:         "title": "Pizza Delivery",
 330:         "subtitle": "Order #456",
 331:         "summary": "Out for delivery ג€” ETA 8 minutes",
 332:     },
 333:     "order_id": "order-456",
 334:     "title": "Pizza Delivery",
 335:     "subtitle": "Order #456 ג€¢ ETA 8 minutes",
 336:     "body": "Driver: Sam. Truck: 7F-12.",
 337: }).encode("utf-8")
 338: 
 339: # AAD the device will verify against on AES-GCM decrypt. `sequence_number`
 340: # stays as a Python int ג€” the canonical JSON emits an integer literal.
 341: aad = assemble_live_card_aad(
 342:     sender_id=client.sender_id,
 343:     user_id=user_id,
 344:     plugin_id=plugin_row_id,
 345:     card_key="order-456",
 346:     sequence_number=2,
 347:     expires_at=expires_at,
 348: )
 349: 
 350: # encrypt_payload is keyword-only, generates a fresh 12-byte nonce
 351: # internally, and returns (nonce, ciphertext_with_tag). Do NOT generate
 352: # your own nonce ג€” using the returned one is mandatory because that's the
 353: # one bound to the ciphertext by AES-GCM.
 354: nonce, ciphertext = encrypt_payload(
 355:     pairing_key=client.pairing_key,
 356:     plaintext=plaintext,
 357:     aad=aad,
 358: )
 359: 
 360: client.upsert_card(
 361:     user_id=user_id,
 362:     plugin_id=plugin_row_id,
 363:     card_key="order-456",
 364:     encrypted_payload=ciphertext,
 365:     nonce=nonce,
 366:     sequence_number=2,
 367:     expires_at=expires_at,
 368: )
 369: ```
 370: 
 371: **`card_key` must equal `card_key_path` resolved on the plaintext.** The manifest's `card_key_path` (declared at publish time, e.g. `"$.order_id"`) is the path the host extracts on decrypt to use as the merge key for this card. The `card_key` you pass to `upsert_card` is what the server stores. If the two disagree, the host's per-card merge breaks and your "live" card behaves like a series of event cards. The server doesn't cross-check the two ג€” enforcement is your responsibility. (V1 validates `card_key_path` only as `startswith("$")`; a future phase will tighten this to the full `$.field(.subfield)*` JSONPath grammar used by template fields.)
 372: 
 373: See `docs/crypto-spec.md ֲ§8` for the exact `assemble_live_card_aad` canonical byte shape.
 374: 
 375: **Server-side gates on upsert** (return 4xx if violated ג€” see ֲ§9):
 376: 
 377: - **Active pairing required.** The `(sender_id, user_id)` pair must have a non-revoked `Pairing` row; otherwise 410. Mirrors the message-send path.
 378: - **Plugin must be active and live-type.** `Plugin.revoked_at IS NULL` and `card_type = "live"`; otherwise 410.
 379: - **TTL window.** `expires_at` must be strictly future (else 400) AND at most 48 hours from now (else 400). The cap is server-enforced and not negotiable.
 380: - **Sequence monotonicity.** New `sequence_number` must be strictly greater than the existing row's; else 409.
 381: - **Rate limit.** Fixed window of 60 upserts per minute per `(sender_id, user_id, card_key)`; else 429. (There's also an IP-bucketed pre-auth limit of 120/min for cheap DoS protection.)
 382: 
 383: The successful response triggers a `card.upsert` SSE event to every active device of the user, so foreground clients refresh within ~1s.
 384: 
 385: #### Deleting a live card
 386: 
 387: ```python
 388: client.delete_card(
 389:     user_id=user_id,
 390:     card_key="order-456",
 391: )
 392: ```
 393: 
 394: `user_id` is **required**. The canonical signed envelope binds `(sender_id, user_id, card_key)` ג€” without `user_id` in the signature, an attacker (or a coincidence: two users with the same `card_key` under the same sender) could be deleted by mistake. The delete endpoint matches exactly that triple in the row lookup.
 395: 
 396: ### 5.5 Revoking a plugin version
 397: 
 398: Revoke a single published plugin row when that exact version should be treated as inactive:
 399: 
 400: ```python

 succeeded in 372ms:
   1: """Sender client ג€” the top-level API for backends sending into Syncler."""
   2: 
   3: from __future__ import annotations
   4: 
   5: import json
   6: import time
   7: import uuid
   8: from dataclasses import dataclass
   9: from datetime import UTC, datetime, timedelta
  10: from typing import Any
  11: 
  12: import requests
  13: from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric.ed25519 import Ed25519PrivateKey
  14: 
  15: 
  16: def _canon_uuid(value: str) -> str:
  17:     """Normalize a UUID string to lowercase no-brace canonical form.
  18: 
  19:     The server stores UUIDs as ``str(uuid.UUID(payload.xxx))`` which always
  20:     lowercases and strips braces. The SDK signs over caller-supplied
  21:     strings, so uppercase or braced inputs would silently mismatch
  22:     (401 invalid signature). Normalize at the boundary.
  23:     """
  24:     return str(uuid.UUID(str(value)))
  25: 
  26: from syncler.preview import HOST_PREVIEW_KEY, validate_host_preview
  27: from syncler.crypto import (
  28:     assemble_envelope,
  29:     b64,
  30:     b64d,
  31:     canonical_json,
  32:     encrypt_payload,
  33:     load_private_key,
  34:     public_key_raw,
  35: )
  36: from syncler.errors import (
  37:     PairingConflictError,
  38:     PairingExpiredError,
  39:     PluginRevokedError,
  40:     RecipientUnreachableError,
  41:     SignatureError,
  42:     SynclerError,
  43: )
  44: 
  45: 
  46: DEFAULT_BASE_URL = "https://api.syncler.app"
  47: 
  48: 
  49: @dataclass
  50: class Pairing:
  51:     pairing_id: str
  52:     user_id: str  # the recipient's user UUID after pairing completes
  53: 
  54: 
  55: @dataclass
  56: class SendResult:
  57:     message_id: str
  58:     expires_at: str
  59: 
  60: 
  61: class Client:
  62:     """Thin sync wrapper over the Syncler server REST API.
  63: 
  64:     Usage::
  65: 
  66:         client = Client(
  67:             base_url="https://api.syncler.app",
  68:             sender_name="Trading Bot",
  69:             private_key_path="~/.syncler/keys/trading.pem",
  70:         )
  71:         client.register_if_needed(contact="ops@example.com")
  72: 
  73:         qr_path = client.create_pairing_qr(ttl_seconds=300)
  74:         pairing = client.wait_for_pairing(timeout_seconds=300)
  75: 
  76:         client.send_to(
  77:             user_uuid=pairing.user_id,
  78:             plugin_identifier="com.trading.app",
  79:             payload={"pnl": 1234.56},
  80:             min_plugin_version="1.0.0",
  81:             # pairing_key produced by the device + sender during the
  82:             # bootstrap exchange (M7+; for V1 dev set client.pairing_key
  83:             # directly with a 32-byte shared secret).
  84:         )
  85:     """
  86: 
  87:     def __init__(
  88:         self,
  89:         *,
  90:         sender_name: str,
  91:         private_key_path: str,
  92:         base_url: str = DEFAULT_BASE_URL,
  93:         session: requests.Session | None = None,
  94:     ):
  95:         self.base_url = base_url.rstrip("/")
  96:         self.sender_name = sender_name
  97:         self.private_key: Ed25519PrivateKey = load_private_key(private_key_path)
  98:         self.public_key = public_key_raw(self.private_key)
  99:         self.session = session or requests.Session()
 100: 
 101:         # State that gets set after register / pairing.
 102:         self.sender_id: str | None = None
 103:         self._pending_pairing_token: str | None = None
 104:         self._latest_pairing: Pairing | None = None
 105:         # In V1 the per-pairing AES-GCM key needs to be exchanged with the
 106:         # user's device during the pairing handshake. Until M7's bootstrap
 107:         # is fully wired, callers can set this directly for dev.
 108:         self.pairing_key: bytes | None = None
 109: 
 110:     # ---------------------------- Sender lifecycle -------------------------
 111: 
 112:     def _canonical_sender_id(self) -> str:
 113:         if self.sender_id is None:
 114:             raise SynclerError("sender_id not set")
 115:         return _canon_uuid(self.sender_id)
 116: 
 117:     def register_if_needed(self, *, contact: str | None = None) -> str:
 118:         """Register the sender public key once. Returns sender_id.
 119: 
 120:         Idempotent: if a server-side row already exists for this public key,
 121:         the server returns 409. The caller is expected to persist
 122:         ``self.sender_id`` between runs; in dev we cache to a JSON file
 123:         beside the private key ג€” but the SDK keeps that detail outside its
 124:         responsibility. For now, the caller catches a 409 themselves.
 125:         """
 126:         body = {
 127:             "public_key": b64(self.public_key),
 128:             "name": self.sender_name,
 129:             "contact": contact,
 130:         }
 131:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/senders/register", json=body, timeout=10)
 132:         if resp.status_code == 409:
 133:             raise SynclerError("sender already registered (use the previously-issued sender_id)")
 134:         resp.raise_for_status()
 135:         self.sender_id = resp.json()["sender_id"]
 136:         return self.sender_id
 137: 
 138:     def set_sender_id(self, sender_id: str) -> None:
 139:         """Set sender_id from a persisted location (after first register)."""
 140:         self.sender_id = sender_id
 141: 
 142:     # ---------------------------- Pairing ----------------------------------
 143: 
 144:     def create_pairing_qr(
 145:         self,
 146:         *,
 147:         ttl_seconds: int = 300,
 148:         metadata: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 149:         out_path: str | None = None,
 150:     ) -> str:
 151:         """Initiate a pairing and write a QR-code PNG of the broker URL.
 152: 
 153:         Returns the path to the generated PNG. Caller is responsible for
 154:         showing the QR to the user.
 155:         """
 156:         self._require_sender_id()
 157:         body = {
 158:             "sender_id": self._canonical_sender_id(),
 159:             "ttl_seconds": ttl_seconds,
 160:             "metadata": metadata or {},
 161:         }
 162:         body["signature"] = b64(self.private_key.sign(canonical_json(body)))
 163:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/pairing/initiate", json=body, timeout=10)
 164:         resp.raise_for_status()
 165:         data = resp.json()
 166:         self._pending_pairing_token = data["pairing_token"]
 167: 
 168:         broker_url = data["broker_url"]
 169:         out_path = out_path or f"syncler-pairing-{int(time.time())}.png"
 170:         _render_qr(broker_url, out_path)
 171:         return out_path
 172: 
 173:     def wait_for_pairing(
 174:         self,
 175:         *,
 176:         timeout_seconds: int = 300,
 177:         poll_interval_seconds: int = 2,
 178:     ) -> Pairing:
 179:         """Poll until the user completes pairing (server holds pending row
 180:         until POST /pairing/complete is called by the user device).
 181: 
 182:         V1 implementation: poll /v1/senders/{sender_id}/pairings (TODO: this
 183:         list endpoint needs to be added server-side). For now this is a
 184:         placeholder that requires the user_id to be supplied out-of-band
 185:         once pairing completes (e.g. the user copies it from the device
 186:         UI). Replace with proper polling once the server endpoint lands.
 187:         """
 188:         # TODO(M11): once a public "did this token complete?" endpoint exists,
 189:         # poll it here. For V1 dev the caller passes user_id manually.
 190:         raise NotImplementedError(
 191:             "wait_for_pairing requires a server endpoint that's part of M11 polish ג€” "
 192:             "for dev use, ask the user for the user_id printed on the device after pairing."
 193:         )
 194: 
 195:     def set_pairing(self, user_id: str, pairing_key: bytes) -> None:
 196:         """Dev-mode shortcut: set the paired user_id and per-pairing AES key.
 197: 
 198:         Production flow has the device exchange this key with the sender
 199:         during the pairing handshake (M7+).
 200:         """
 201:         if len(pairing_key) != 32:
 202:             raise ValueError("pairing_key must be 32 bytes")
 203:         self._latest_pairing = Pairing(pairing_id="", user_id=user_id)
 204:         self.pairing_key = pairing_key
 205: 
 206:     # ---------------------------- Sending ----------------------------------
 207: 
 208:     def send_to(
 209:         self,
 210:         *,
 211:         user_uuid: str,
 212:         plugin_identifier: str,
 213:         plugin_id: str,
 214:         payload: dict[str, Any],
 215:         min_plugin_version: str = "",
 216:         ttl_seconds: int = 7 * 24 * 3600,
 217:     ) -> SendResult:
 218:         # Canonicalize UUIDs so signature bytes match server reconstruction.
 219:         user_uuid = _canon_uuid(user_uuid)
 220:         plugin_id = _canon_uuid(plugin_id)
 221:         """Encrypt the payload, sign the envelope, POST to /messages/send.
 222: 
 223:         ``plugin_id`` is the row-UUID of a specific published version (from
 224:         ``client.publish_plugin``'s return), NOT the plugin_identifier.
 225:         ``plugin_identifier`` is the stable sender-chosen string.
 226:         """
 227:         self._require_sender_id()
 228:         if self.pairing_key is None:
 229:             raise SynclerError("no pairing key set; call set_pairing() first")
 230: 
 231:         # Validate the optional hostPreview block in the payload. The host
 232:         # uses it to render the inbox row natively without invoking the
 233:         # plugin. Missing block ג†’ fallback row; malformed block ג†’ raises so
 234:         # the sender catches the mistake at send time rather than the user
 235:         # seeing "New message from X" with no detail.
 236:         if HOST_PREVIEW_KEY in payload:
 237:             validate_host_preview(payload[HOST_PREVIEW_KEY])
 238: 
 239:         expires_at = (datetime.now(UTC) + timedelta(seconds=ttl_seconds)).isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z")
 240:         plaintext = json.dumps(payload, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8")
 241: 
 242:         nonce, ciphertext = encrypt_payload(
 243:             pairing_key=self.pairing_key,
 244:             plaintext=plaintext,
 245:             aad=_aad(
 246:                 sender_id=self._canonical_sender_id(),
 247:                 user_id=user_uuid,
 248:                 plugin_id=plugin_id,
 249:                 min_plugin_version=min_plugin_version,
 250:                 expires_at=expires_at,
 251:             ),
 252:         )
 253:         encrypted_body_b64 = b64(ciphertext)
 254:         nonce_b64 = b64(nonce)
 255: 
 256:         envelope = assemble_envelope(
 257:             sender_id=self._canonical_sender_id(),
 258:             user_id=user_uuid,
 259:             plugin_id=plugin_id,
 260:             min_plugin_version=min_plugin_version,
 261:             expires_at=expires_at,
 262:             encrypted_body_b64=encrypted_body_b64,
 263:             nonce_b64=nonce_b64,
 264:         )
 265:         signature = self.private_key.sign(envelope)
 266: 
 267:         body = {
 268:             "sender_id": self._canonical_sender_id(),
 269:             "user_id": user_uuid,
 270:             "plugin_id": plugin_id,
 271:             "encrypted_body": encrypted_body_b64,
 272:             "nonce": nonce_b64,
 273:             "envelope_signature": b64(signature),
 274:             "min_plugin_version": min_plugin_version or None,
 275:             "expires_at": expires_at,
 276:         }
 277: 
 278:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/messages/send", json=body, timeout=10)
 279:         if resp.status_code == 401:
 280:             raise SignatureError("server rejected envelope signature")
 281:         if resp.status_code == 410:
 282:             detail = resp.json().get("detail", "")
 283:             if "plugin" in detail:
 284:                 raise PluginRevokedError(detail)
 285:             raise RecipientUnreachableError(detail or "recipient unreachable")
 286:         if resp.status_code == 409:
 287:             raise SynclerError("nonce replay or pairing conflict")
 288:         resp.raise_for_status()
 289:         data = resp.json()
 290:         return SendResult(message_id=data["message_id"], expires_at=data["expires_at"])
 291: 
 292:     # ---------------------------- Plugin publishing ------------------------
 293: 
 294:     def publish_plugin(
 295:         self,
 296:         *,
 297:         plugin_identifier: str,
 298:         version: str,
 299:         manifest_hash: bytes,
 300:         bundle_hash: bytes,
 301:         bundle_signature: bytes,
 302:         signed_bundle_url: str,
 303:         capabilities: list[str],
 304:         endpoints: list[str],
 305:         renderer: str = "script",
 306:         template: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 307:         card_type: str = "event",
 308:         card_key_path: str | None = None,
 309:     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 310:         """Publish a new plugin version. Returns the server response (with
 311:         ``plugin_row_id`` which the sender then uses in messages).
 312: 
 313:         Phase 3a: pass ``renderer="template"`` plus a ``template`` block to
 314:         ship a native Compose-rendered card instead of a WebView bundle.
 315: 
 316:         Phase 3b: pass ``card_type="live"`` plus a ``card_key_path`` (JSONPath
 317:         yielding the stable key for the card) to enable persistent,
 318:         upsertable live cards.
 319:         """
 320:         self._require_sender_id()
 321:         body: dict[str, Any] = {
 322:             "sender_id": self._canonical_sender_id(),
 323:             "plugin_identifier": plugin_identifier,
 324:             "version": version,
 325:             "manifest_hash": b64(manifest_hash),
 326:             "bundle_hash": b64(bundle_hash),
 327:             "signature": b64(bundle_signature),
 328:             "signed_bundle_url": signed_bundle_url,
 329:             "capabilities": capabilities,
 330:             "endpoints": endpoints,
 331:         }
 332:         # Mirror the server's `_publish_envelope` conditional inclusion.
 333:         if renderer != "script":
 334:             body["renderer"] = renderer
 335:         if template is not None:
 336:             body["template"] = template
 337:         if card_type != "event":
 338:             body["card_type"] = card_type
 339:         if card_key_path is not None:
 340:             body["card_key_path"] = card_key_path
 341: 
 342:         body["sender_signature"] = b64(self.private_key.sign(canonical_json(body)))
 343:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/plugins/publish", json=body, timeout=10)
 344:         resp.raise_for_status()
 345:         return resp.json()
 346: 
 347:     def upsert_card(
 348:         self,
 349:         *,
 350:         user_id: str,
 351:         plugin_id: str,
 352:         card_key: str,
 353:         encrypted_payload: bytes,
 354:         nonce: bytes,
 355:         sequence_number: int,
 356:         expires_at: datetime,
 357:     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 358:         """Upsert a persistent live card for a user. Fires card.upsert SSE.
 359: 
 360:         UUIDs are normalized via [_canon_uuid] before signing so an uppercase
 361:         or braced caller input produces the same canonical bytes as the
 362:         server-side `str(uuid.UUID(...))` form. Without this, a sender-side
 363:         self-401 can sneak in on UUIDs that look fine to the eye but
 364:         differ in case (Codex consultation 63 YELLOW follow-up).
 365:         """
 366:         self._require_sender_id()
 367:         body: dict[str, Any] = {
 368:             "sender_id": self._canonical_sender_id(),
 369:             "user_id": _canon_uuid(user_id),
 370:             "plugin_id": _canon_uuid(plugin_id),
 371:             "card_key": card_key,
 372:             "encrypted_payload": b64(encrypted_payload),
 373:             "nonce": b64(nonce),
 374:             "sequence_number": sequence_number,
 375:             "expires_at": expires_at.isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z"),
 376:         }
 377: 
 378:         # Envelope for upsert includes card_type: live. `sequence_number`
 379:         # stays as int here to match the server's canonical envelope
 380:         # (see routers/cards.py:_build_upsert_envelope_bytes).
 381:         envelope = dict(body)
 382:         envelope["card_type"] = "live"
 383:         body["envelope_signature"] = b64(self.private_key.sign(canonical_json(envelope)))
 384: 
 385:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/cards/upsert", json=body, timeout=10)
 386:         resp.raise_for_status()
 387:         return resp.json()
 388: 
 389:     def delete_card(
 390:         self,
 391:         *,
 392:         user_id: str,
 393:         card_key: str,
 394:     ) -> None:
 395:         """Delete a persistent live card for a specific user. Fires card.delete SSE.
 396: 
 397:         Phase 3b: `user_id` is REQUIRED in the canonical signed envelope so a
 398:         delete signature for one user's card cannot be replayed against
 399:         another user's card with the same (sender, card_key). Mirrors the
 400:         server's `_build_delete_envelope_bytes`. Closes Codex consultation
 401:         62 RED #5.
 402:         """
 403:         self._require_sender_id()
 404:         sender_id = self._canonical_sender_id()
 405:         user_id_canonical = _canon_uuid(user_id)
 406:         envelope = canonical_json(
 407:             {
 408:                 "sender_id": sender_id,
 409:                 "user_id": user_id_canonical,
 410:                 "card_key": card_key,
 411:             }
 412:         )
 413:         body = {
 414:             "sender_id": sender_id,
 415:             "user_id": user_id_canonical,
 416:             "card_key": card_key,
 417:             "envelope_signature": b64(self.private_key.sign(envelope)),
 418:         }
 419:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/cards/delete", json=body, timeout=10)
 420:         resp.raise_for_status()

 422:     # Accepted classifications for the optional ``reason`` field on revoke.
 423:     # The host renders different UX per reason: silent for ``superseded``,
 424:     # security alert with refuse-to-execute for ``compromised``, neutral
 425:     # "no longer available" banner for ``sender_disabled``. ``unspecified``
 426:     # is the conservative default for legacy revokes with no reason given;
 427:     # callers SHOULD always supply a real classification.

 181:     *,

 184:     since: datetime | None,
 185:     limit: int = 50,
 186: ) -> tuple[list[Message], datetime | None]:
 187:     now = datetime.now(UTC)
 188:     # Phase 2 carry-over (Codex consultation 57 YELLOW, Phase 3a delivery):
 189:     # LEFT OUTER JOIN the per-device delivery status so we can filter out
 190:     # messages this device has already dismissed. When no DeliveryStatus row
 191:     # exists for (message, device), the join returns NULL ג€” `IS NULL` keeps
 192:     # those rows. When a row exists with `dismissed_at IS NOT NULL`, the
 193:     # filter drops it, which is what makes cross-device dismiss visible on
 194:     # the next pull (and on the `dismiss` SSE event's repository.refresh).
 195:     query = (
 196:         select(Message)
 197:         .outerjoin(
 198:             DeliveryStatus,
 199:             and_(
 200:                 DeliveryStatus.message_id == Message.id,
 201:                 DeliveryStatus.device_id == device_id,
 202:             ),

 205:             and_(
 206:                 Message.user_id == user_id,
 207:                 Message.expires_at > now,
 208:                 DeliveryStatus.dismissed_at.is_(None),
 209:             ),
 210:         )
 211:         .order_by(Message.sent_at.asc())
 212:         .limit(limit)
 213:     )
 214:     if since is not None:
 215:         query = query.where(Message.sent_at > since)
 216: 
 217:     result = await db.execute(query)
 218:     messages = list(result.scalars().all())
 219:     next_since = messages[-1].sent_at if messages else since
 220:     return messages, next_since

 553:     @model_validator(mode="after")
 554:     def validate_renderer_template_pairing(self) -> "PluginPublishRequest":
 555:         # The pairing rules live here (not on TemplateObject) because the
 556:         # action-endpoint check needs the surrounding `endpoints` glob list.
 557:         if self.renderer == "template" and self.template is None:
 558:             raise ValueError("template required when renderer == 'template'")
 559:         if self.renderer == "script" and self.template is not None:
 560:             raise ValueError("template must be omitted when renderer == 'script'")
 561:         if self.template is not None:
 562:             for action in self.template.actions:
 563:                 if not any(
 564:                     _endpoint_pattern_matches(action.endpoint, p)
 565:                     for p in self.endpoints
 566:                 ):
 567:                     raise ValueError(
 568:                         f"action {action.id!r} endpoint {action.endpoint!r} "
 569:                         f"not allowed by declared endpoints",
 570:                     )
 571:         # Phase 3b: live cards MUST have a card_key_path to extract their
 572:         # stable identity from the payload.
 573:         if self.card_type == "live" and not self.card_key_path:
 574:             raise ValueError("card_key_path required when card_type == 'live'")
 575:         return self

  42:     return base64.b64encode(value).decode("ascii")

  45: def _build_upsert_envelope_bytes(payload: LiveCardUpsertRequest) -> bytes:
  46:     """Build the canonical envelope for live card upsert (binds metadata).
  47: 
  48:     `sequence_number` is kept as an int (not stringified) so the canonical
  49:     form matches the SDK side, which signs `canonical_json` of a dict whose
  50:     `sequence_number` is also int. Casting to str here would emit
  51:     `"sequence_number":"42"` while the SDK emits `"sequence_number":42`,
  52:     breaking signature verification on every upsert.
  53:     """
  54:     return assemble_envelope(
  55:         {
  56:             "sender_id": str(payload.sender_id),
  57:             "user_id": str(payload.user_id),
  58:             "plugin_id": str(payload.plugin_id),
  59:             "card_key": payload.card_key,
  60:             "card_type": "live",
  61:             "expires_at": payload.expires_at.isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z"),
  62:             "encrypted_payload": payload.encrypted_payload,
  63:             "nonce": payload.nonce,
  64:             "sequence_number": payload.sequence_number,
  65:         }
  66:     )
  67:

  69: @router.post("/upsert", status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
  70: async def upsert(
  71:     payload: LiveCardUpsertRequest,
  72:     request: Request,
  73:     _: None = Depends(rate_limit("card_upsert_ip")),
  74:     db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db),
  75: ) -> LiveCardItem:
  76:     try:
  77:         sender: Sender = await get_active_sender(db, payload.sender_id)
  78:     except SenderNotFoundError as exc:
  79:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND, detail="sender not found") from exc
  80:     except SenderRevokedError as exc:
  81:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_410_GONE, detail="sender revoked") from exc
  82: 
  83:     envelope_bytes = _build_upsert_envelope_bytes(payload)
  84:     signature = decode_base64(payload.envelope_signature, field_name="envelope_signature", exact=64)
  85: 
  86:     if not verify_message_envelope(sender.public_key, envelope_bytes, signature):
  87:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED, detail="invalid envelope signature")
  88: 
  89:     # Per-card rate limit: 1 per second per (sender, user, card_key).
  90:     request.state.sender_id = str(payload.sender_id)
  91:     request.state.user_id = str(payload.user_id)
  92:     request.state.card_key = payload.card_key
  93:     from app.middleware.rate_limit import check_rate_limit
  94:     from app.middleware.rate_limit_config import RATE_LIMITS
  95:     await check_rate_limit(db, request, RATE_LIMITS["card_upsert"])
  96: 
  97:     try:
  98:         card = await upsert_live_card(
  99:             db,
 100:             sender_id=payload.sender_id,
 101:             user_id=payload.user_id,
 102:             plugin_id=payload.plugin_id,
 103:             card_key=payload.card_key,
 104:             encrypted_payload=decode_base64(payload.encrypted_payload, field_name="encrypted_payload", minimum=16),
 105:             nonce=decode_base64(payload.nonce, field_name="nonce", exact=12),
 106:             sequence_number=payload.sequence_number,
 107:             expires_at=payload.expires_at,
 108:         )
 109:     except PluginInactiveError as exc:
 110:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_410_GONE, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 111:     except PairingMissingError as exc:
 112:         # Mirrors the messages route: no active pairing ג†’ 410 Gone. The
 113:         # sender knows what to do (re-pair) and we don't leak whether the
 114:         # user_id exists at all (404 vs 410 would differ).
 115:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_410_GONE, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 116:     except ExpiredEnvelopeError as exc:
 117:         # expires_at <= now OR exceeds the 48h server-enforced cap. 400 Bad
 118:         # Request ג€” the caller can fix and resubmit. Closes Codex 63 RED
 119:         # (router-layer mapping for the service-layer TTL check).
 120:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 121:     except SequenceNumberRegressionError as exc:
 122:         raise HTTPException(status_code=status.HTTP_409_CONFLICT, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 123: 
 124:     # SSE fanout
 125:     from app.models import Plugin
 126:     from sqlalchemy import select as sql_select
 127:     plugin_row = await db.execute(sql_select(Plugin.plugin_identifier).where(Plugin.id == card.plugin_id))
 128:     identifier = plugin_row.scalar_one_or_none() or ""
 129: 
 130:     item = LiveCardItem(
 131:         id=card.id,
 132:         sender_id=card.sender_id,
 133:         plugin_id=card.plugin_id,
 134:         plugin_identifier=identifier,
 135:         card_key=card.card_key,
 136:         encrypted_payload=_b64(card.encrypted_payload),
 137:         nonce=_b64(card.nonce),
 138:         sequence_number=card.sequence_number,
 139:         updated_at=card.updated_at,
 140:         expires_at=card.expires_at,
 141:     )
 142:     
 143:     await get_event_bus().publish_to_user(
 144:         user_id=card.user_id,
 145:         event_type="card.upsert",
 146:         data=item.model_dump(mode="json"),
 147:     )
 148:     
 149:     return item

 152: def _build_delete_envelope_bytes(payload: LiveCardDeleteRequest) -> bytes:
 153:     """Canonical envelope for live card delete (Codex consultation 62 RED #5).
 154: 
 155:     Binds `user_id` so a delete signature for one user's card cannot be
 156:     replayed against another user's card with the same (sender, card_key).
 157:     Uses the same `assemble_envelope` canonicalization as the upsert path
 158:     so signing libraries on the sender side stay consistent across the
 159:     two routes.
 160:     """
 161:     return assemble_envelope(
 162:         {
 163:             "sender_id": str(payload.sender_id),
 164:             "user_id": str(payload.user_id),
 165:             "card_key": payload.card_key,
 166:         }
 167:     )

  10: 
  11: from app.models import LiveCard, Pairing, Plugin
  12: 
  13: # Server-enforced 48h TTL ceiling. Sender-supplied `expires_at` is clamped
  14: # against `now + MAX_TTL` so a malicious or buggy sender can't squat a card
  15: # slot indefinitely (Codex consultation 62 RED #4). Aligns with the Phase 3b
  16: # plan in .triad/50-agreement-and-plan.md.
  17: MAX_TTL = timedelta(hours=48)
  18: 
  19: 
  20: class CardError(Exception):
  21:     """Base class for card service errors."""
  22: 
  23: 
  24: class CardNotFoundError(CardError):
  25:     """Card not found."""
  26: 
  27: 
  28: class PluginInactiveError(CardError):
  29:     """Plugin missing, revoked, or not owned by sender."""
  30: 
  31: 
  32: class PairingMissingError(CardError):
  33:     """No active (sender_id, user_id) pairing."""
  34: 
  35: 
  36: class ExpiredEnvelopeError(CardError):
  37:     """expires_at is not in the future or exceeds the server-enforced cap."""
  38: 
  39: 
  40: class SequenceNumberRegressionError(CardError):
  41:     """New sequence number is not greater than existing."""
  42: 
  43: 
  44: async def upsert_live_card(
  45:     db: AsyncSession,
  46:     *,
  47:     sender_id: uuid.UUID,
  48:     user_id: uuid.UUID,
  49:     plugin_id: uuid.UUID,
  50:     card_key: str,
  51:     encrypted_payload: bytes,
  52:     nonce: bytes,
  53:     sequence_number: int,
  54:     expires_at: datetime,
  55: ) -> LiveCard:
  56:     now = datetime.now(UTC)
  57:     # TTL enforcement (Codex consultation 62 RED #4): reject already-expired
  58:     # expires_at and clamp anything beyond the 48h cap. Mirrors the
  59:     # `store_message` MAX_RETENTION pattern in services/messages.py.
  60:     if expires_at <= now:
  61:         raise ExpiredEnvelopeError("expires_at is not in the future")
  62:     if expires_at > now + MAX_TTL:
  63:         raise ExpiredEnvelopeError(
  64:             f"expires_at exceeds the {int(MAX_TTL.total_seconds() // 3600)}h live-card cap"
  65:         )
  66: 
  67:     # Pairing check (Codex consultation 62 RED #3): live-card upsert MUST
  68:     # require an active (sender_id, user_id) pairing, same as the message
  69:     # store path. Without this, any registered sender could push live cards
  70:     # to any user they happen to know the UUID of.
  71:     pairing_result = await db.execute(
  72:         select(Pairing).where(
  73:             and_(
  74:                 Pairing.sender_id == sender_id,
  75:                 Pairing.user_id == user_id,
  76:                 Pairing.revoked_at.is_(None),
  77:             ),
  78:         ),
  79:     )
  80:     if pairing_result.scalar_one_or_none() is None:
  81:         raise PairingMissingError("no active pairing")
  82: 
  83:     # Plugin lookup (Codex consultation 62 RED #2): include the
  84:     # `Plugin.revoked_at.is_(None)` filter so revoked plugins cannot upsert
  85:     # live cards (matches the messages service `_plugin` pattern).
  86:     result = await db.execute(
  87:         select(Plugin).where(
  88:             and_(
  89:                 Plugin.id == plugin_id,
  90:                 Plugin.sender_id == sender_id,
  91:                 Plugin.card_type == "live",
  92:                 Plugin.revoked_at.is_(None),
  93:             )
  94:         )
  95:     )
  96:     plugin = result.scalar_one_or_none()
  97:     if plugin is None:
  98:         raise PluginInactiveError(
  99:             "plugin missing, revoked, not live-type, or not owned by sender"
 100:         )
 101: 
 102:     # 2. Upsert with sequence number check.
 103:     existing_result = await db.execute(
 104:         select(LiveCard).where(
 105:             and_(
 106:                 LiveCard.sender_id == sender_id,
 107:                 LiveCard.user_id == user_id,
 108:                 LiveCard.card_key == card_key,
 109:             )
 110:         )
 111:     )
 112:     existing = existing_result.scalar_one_or_none()
 113:     
 114:     now = datetime.now(UTC)
 115:     if existing:
 116:         if sequence_number <= existing.sequence_number:
 117:             raise SequenceNumberRegressionError(
 118:                 f"sequence_number {sequence_number} not greater than {existing.sequence_number}"
 119:             )
 120:         
 121:         existing.encrypted_payload = encrypted_payload
 122:         existing.nonce = nonce
 123:         existing.sequence_number = sequence_number
 124:         existing.updated_at = now
 125:         existing.expires_at = expires_at

 246: Canonical JSON for the sender's `envelope_signature` on `POST /v1/cards/upsert`:
 247: 
 248: ```json
 249: {
 250:   "card_key": "...",
 251:   "card_type": "live",
 252:   "encrypted_payload": "<base64 ciphertext_with_tag, no nonce prefix>",
 253:   "expires_at": "<ISO8601 UTC with Z suffix>",
 254:   "nonce": "<base64 12-byte nonce>",
 255:   "plugin_id": "...",
 256:   "sender_id": "...",
 257:   "sequence_number": <integer JSON literal>,
 258:   "user_id": "..."
 259: }
 260: ```
 261: 
 262: The server constructs the same canonical bytes from the request body (via `assemble_envelope` in `server/app/routers/cards.py`) and verifies against the registered sender's public key. UUIDs MUST be canonicalized to lowercase no-brace form before signing (`str(uuid.UUID(value))`) ג€” the SDK normalizes via `_canon_uuid` to prevent sender-side self-401s on uppercase or braced input.
 263: 
 264: ### 8.3 Live Card Delete Envelope (Ed25519 signing input)
 265: 
 266: Canonical JSON for `POST /v1/cards/delete`:
 267: 
 268: ```json
 269: {
 270:   "card_key": "...",
 271:   "sender_id": "...",
 272:   "user_id": "..."
 273: }
 274: ```
 275: 
 276: **`user_id` is REQUIRED in the envelope.** Without it, a delete signature valid for one user's card could be replayed against another user's card with a coincidentally matching `(sender_id, card_key)` ג€” the table is uniquely keyed on `(sender_id, user_id, card_key)`, so the lookup would otherwise be ambiguous. (Codex consultation 62 security finding.) The server matches the exact triple before deleting; mismatched triples no-op silently and still publish a `card.delete` SSE event so all of the user's devices clear any stale local copy.
 277: 
 278: ### 8.4 Test Vectors
 279: 
 280: Live-card vectors live alongside the rest in `server/tests/test_crypto.py` (round-trip) and `android/core/crypto/.../SpecVectorsTest.kt` (Android cross-check). The canonical envelope bytes for upsert/delete are asserted in `server/tests/test_phase3.py` via signature-verification round trips against `app/routers/cards.py:_build_upsert_envelope_bytes` and `_build_delete_envelope_bytes`.

 287: from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes
 288: from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers.aead import AESGCM
 289: from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.hkdf import HKDF
 290: 
 291: def derive_pairing_key(master_key: bytes, sender_id: bytes) -> bytes:
 292:     return HKDF(
 293:         algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
 294:         length=32,
 295:         salt=sender_id,
 296:         info=b"syncler-v1-pairing-key:" + sender_id,
 297:     ).derive(master_key)
 298: 
 299: def assemble_aad(fields: dict[str, object]) -> bytes:
 300:     return json.dumps(fields, ensure_ascii=True, separators=(",", ":"), sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")
 301: 
 302: def decrypt(pairing_key: bytes, wire: bytes, aad: bytes) -> bytes:
 303:     nonce = wire[:12]
 304:     ciphertext_with_tag = wire[12:]
 305:     return AESGCM(pairing_key).decrypt(nonce, ciphertext_with_tag, aad)
 306: 
 307: # --- Live cards (ֲ§8) -----------------------------------------------------
 308: 
 309: def _canon_uuid(value) -> str:
 310:     """Normalize a UUID to the lowercase no-brace form the server stores
 311:     via str(uuid.UUID(payload.*)). Required before signing: uppercase or
 312:     braced input from a caller would otherwise produce a canonical-bytes
 313:     mismatch and a self-401 from the server."""
 314:     return str(uuid.UUID(str(value)))
 315:

 324: ) -> bytes:

 326:         {
 327:             "card_key": card_key,
 328:             "card_type": "live",
 329:             "expires_at": expires_at.isoformat().replace("+00:00", "Z"),
 330:             "plugin_id": _canon_uuid(plugin_id),
 331:             "sender_id": _canon_uuid(sender_id),
 332:             "user_id": _canon_uuid(user_id),
 333:             "sequence_number": sequence_number,
 334:         },
 335:         ensure_ascii=True,
 336:         separators=(",", ":"),
 337:         sort_keys=True,
 338:     ).encode("utf-8")

   1: # Syncler Roadmap
   2: 
   3: The Syncler platform is built and released in milestones. **V1 is what ships today**; the items below it are sequenced by platform dependencies (security primitives first, capability surface second, scaling third, UX last).
   4: 
   5: This file is the public roadmap. Internal implementation phases (Phase 0 / 1 / 2 / 3 / 4) used in the codebase and consultations track *how V1 was built*; this document tracks *what comes next*.
   6: 
   7: ## V1 ג€” Foundational milestone (shipped)
   8: 
   9: - [x] Device-bound JWTs with server-side revocation enforcement
  10: - [x] Synced pairing via the encrypted user-state blob (M7 CAS state)
  11: - [x] Server-Sent Events stream for real-time hint delivery (`inbox.changed`, `state.changed`, `dismiss`, `card.upsert`, `card.delete`)
  12: - [x] Native Material 3 template renderer (no-JS plugins via JSONPath manifest)
  13: - [x] Persistent, upsertable Live Cards with server-enforced 48h TTL + sequence-monotone updates
  14: - [x] Host-owned plugin settings sheet (sender mute, pairing revoke). Sender-side plugin-row revoke (`client.revoke_plugin(...)`) is a separate published-side API; the host UI exposes pairing revoke, not plugin-row revoke.
  15: - [x] Cross-device dismiss filter (server-side `DeliveryStatus` join)
  16: - [x] Per-device envelope auth-token isolation for template-renderer action POSTs
  17: 
  18: ## V1.5 ג€” Plugin runtime + key hygiene
  19: 
  20: 1. **Multi-process plugin host.** Move JS plugin execution to a dedicated Android process via AIDL/Binder. Isolates a crashing or runaway plugin from the host UI process and gives us a clean ProcessRecord boundary for the OS to kill independently.
  21: 2. **Native Kotlin plugin runtime (out-of-process).** A second plugin format alongside the JS bundle: a signed AAR loaded into the isolated process. Performance + platform-API parity for plugin authors who want a native experience, with the IPC boundary preventing in-process ClassLoader poisoning.
  22: 3. **Master-key rotation.** UX + protocol for rotating the user's 32-byte master key without losing access to historical state. Required before per-device encryption (#4) lands.
  23: 4. **Per-device envelope encryption.** Senders encrypt the payload separately for each of the user's enrolled devices, keyed by per-device public keys instead of the shared user master key. Enables forward secrecy and immediate per-device revocation without rotating user-wide keys.
  24: 5. **Durable nonce-replay protection.** Move the per-sender nonce registry from in-memory to Postgres so a worker restart can't accept a replayed envelope.
  25:

  77: 
  78: def _revoke_envelope(payload: PluginRevokeRequest) -> bytes:
  79:     # Canonical 3-field envelope. Reason is part of the signed bytes so a
  80:     # man-in-the-middle can't strip a "compromised" reason down to a silent
  81:     # "superseded". Backwards compat with M8.1 clients: when reason is None
  82:     # we omit it from the envelope so the signature shape matches.
  83:     envelope: dict[str, str] = {
  84:         "sender_id": str(payload.sender_id),
  85:         "plugin_row_id": str(payload.plugin_row_id),
  86:     }
  87:     if payload.reason is not None:
  88:         envelope["reason"] = payload.reason
  89:     return json.dumps(envelope, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8")
  90: 
  91: 
  92: @router.post("/publish", response_model=PluginPublishResponse, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
  93: async def publish(
  94:     payload: PluginPublishRequest,
  95:     request: Request,
  96:     # Pre-auth IP bucket ג€” cheap, prevents body-parsing DoS from anonymous
  97:     # callers. The per-sender bucket is applied below, after sig verification.
  98:     _: None = Depends(rate_limit("message_send_ip")),
  99:     db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db),
 100: ) -> PluginPublishResponse:
 101:     try:
 102:         sender = await get_active_sender(db, payload.sender_id)
 103:     except SenderNotFoundError as exc:
 104:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="sender not found") from exc
 105:     except SenderRevokedError as exc:
 106:         raise HTTPException(status_code=410, detail="sender revoked") from exc
 107: 
 108:     sender_sig = decode_base64(payload.sender_signature, field_name="sender_signature", exact=64)
 109:     if not verify_message_envelope(sender.public_key, _publish_envelope(payload), sender_sig):
 110:         raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="invalid sender signature")
 111: 
 112:     # Per-sender bucket AFTER signature verification ג€” a spoofer cannot inflate
 113:     # someone else's bucket by setting a foreign sender_id in the body, because
 114:     # they cannot forge the matching Ed25519 signature.
 115:     request.state.sender_id = str(payload.sender_id)
 116:     await check_rate_limit(db, request, RATE_LIMITS["plugin_publish"])
 117: 
 118:     try:
 119:         plugin = await publish_plugin(
 120:             db,
 121:             sender_id=sender.id,
 122:             plugin_identifier=payload.plugin_identifier,
 123:             version=payload.version,
 124:             manifest_hash=decode_base64(payload.manifest_hash, field_name="manifest_hash", exact=32),
 125:             bundle_hash=decode_base64(payload.bundle_hash, field_name="bundle_hash", exact=32),
 126:             signature=decode_base64(payload.signature, field_name="signature", exact=64),
 127:             signed_bundle_url=payload.signed_bundle_url,
 128:             capabilities=payload.capabilities,
 129:             endpoints=payload.endpoints,
 130:             renderer=payload.renderer,
 131:             template=(payload.template.model_dump(mode="json") if payload.template else None),
 132:             card_type=payload.card_type,
 133:             card_key_path=payload.card_key_path,
 134:         )
 135:     except InvalidVersionError as exc:
 136:         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 137:     except VersionRegressionError as exc:

  type PluginManifest,

  PlatformError,

  type ShowNotificationOptions,

export { storage } from './storage';
export {
  HOST_PREVIEW_KEY,
  HOST_PREVIEW_LIMITS,
  HostPreviewValidationError,
  validateHostPreview,
  type HostPreview,
} from './preview';

/**
 * Type-safe SDK wrapper around the host-injected `window.platform` bridge.
 */
export const platform = {
  /** Shows a host notification. */
  showNotification: showNotificationApi,
  /** Typed key/value storage wrapper. */
  storage: storageApi,
  /** Typed network wrapper with manifest endpoint enforcement. */
  network: networkApi,
  /** Typed notification helper namespace. */
  notifications: notificationsApi,
  /** Camera APIs exposed by the host bridge. */
  camera: {
    /** Captures an image through the host camera UI. */
    capture(opts?: CameraCaptureOptions) {
      return callPlatform('camera.capture', (bridge) => bridge.camera.capture(opts));
    },
  },
  /** Gallery APIs exposed by the host bridge. */
  gallery: {
    /** Picks one or more gallery items through the host UI. */
    pick(opts?: GalleryPickOptions) {
      return callPlatform('gallery.pick', (bridge) => bridge.gallery.pick(opts));
    },
  },
  /** File APIs exposed by the host bridge. */
  file: {
    /** Picks a file through the host UI. */
    pick(opts?: FilePickOptions) {
      return callPlatform('file.pick', (bridge) => bridge.file.pick(opts));
    },
  },
  /** Location APIs exposed by the host bridge. */
  location: {
    /** Reads the current location through the host bridge. */
    current(opts?: LocationCurrentOptions) {
      return callPlatform('location.current', (bridge) => bridge.location.current(opts));
    },
  },
  /** Message response APIs exposed by the host bridge. */
  message: {
    /** Sends an action response payload back through the host bridge. */
    respond(actionId: string, payload: unknown) {
      return callPlatform('message.respond', (bridge) => bridge.message.respond(actionId, payload));
    },
    /** Sets host dismiss behavior for the active message. */
    dismissBehavior(behavior: DismissBehavior) {
      return callPlatformSync('message.dismissBehavior', (bridge) => bridge.message.dismissBehavior(behavior));
    },
  },
  /** Host bridge version. */
  get version() {
    return getPlatformBridge().__version__;
  },
};

 succeeded in 281ms:
  76: ### Action callback (user -> your backend)
  77: 
  78: When the user taps an action button in your plugin, the plugin POSTs to your declared endpoint with whatever body your `onclick` handler builds:
  79: 
  80: ```
  81: POST https://your-app.example.com/api/action
  82: Content-Type: application/json
  83: 
  84: {
  85:   "item_id": "...",
  86:   "acted_at": "2026-05-20T14:30:00Z"
  87: }
  88: ```
  89: 
  90: The platform does **not** inject `device_id` into the body in V1 ג€” see ֲ§7 for the full contract. Idempotency is your responsibility: dedupe by `item_id` (or a sender-generated identifier you echo back) because the platform may double-deliver under retry.
  91: 
  92: ## 3. Plugin code
  93: 
  94: `src/plugin.ts`:

  30: def decrypt_message_body(pairing_key: bytes, wire: bytes, aad: bytes) -> bytes:
  31:     """Decrypt a packed AES-GCM message body."""
  32: 
  33:     if len(pairing_key) != AES_256_KEY_BYTES:
  34:         raise ValueError("pairing_key must be 32 bytes")
  35:     if len(wire) < AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES + AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES:
  36:         raise ValueError("wire is too short")
  37: 
  38:     nonce = wire[:AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES]
  39:     ciphertext_with_tag = wire[AES_GCM_NONCE_BYTES:]
  40:     return AESGCM(pairing_key).decrypt(nonce, ciphertext_with_tag, aad)
  41: 
  42: 
  43: def assemble_aad(fields: dict[str, Any]) -> bytes:
  44:     """Assemble canonical JSON AAD for AES-GCM encryption.
  45: 
  46:     AAD authenticates the protocol context bound to the ciphertext but does
  47:     NOT include the ciphertext itself. See ``assemble_envelope`` for the
  48:     Ed25519 signing input.
  49:     """
  50:     return _canonical(fields)
  51: 
  52: 
  53: def assemble_envelope(fields: dict[str, Any]) -> bytes:
  54:     """Assemble canonical envelope JSON for Ed25519 sender signing.
  55: 
  56:     Envelope = AAD + ``encrypted_body`` (base64) + ``nonce`` (base64).
  57:     """

import { Capability, DismissBehavior } from './enums';
/**
 * One template field ג€” a JSONPath into the decrypted payload. V1 dialect is
 * `$.field(.subfield)*` only (no array indexing, wildcards, or filters).
 */
export interface TemplateField {
    path: string;
}
/**
 * One template action button. `endpoint` MUST match one of the plugin's
 * `declaredEndpoints` globs (validated server-side at publish time).
 */
export interface TemplateAction {
    id: string;
    label: string;
    endpoint: string;
}
/**
 * Template manifest block. Required when `renderer === 'template'`.
 */
export interface TemplateBlock {
    layout: 'standard_card';
    fields: Record<string, TemplateField>;
    actions?: TemplateAction[];
}
/**
 * Plugin metadata consumed by the native host before loading a bundle.
 */
export interface PluginManifest {
    /** Reverse-DNS plugin identifier, for example `com.example.plugin`. */
    id: string;
    /** Human-readable plugin name. */
    name: string;
    /** Semantic plugin version. */
    version: string;
    /** Sender identifier associated with inbound encrypted messages. */
    senderId: string;
    /** Lowercase or uppercase hexadecimal hash of the JavaScript bundle. */
    bundleHash: string;
    /** Lowercase or uppercase hexadecimal Ed25519 signature. */
    signature: string;
    /** Capabilities the plugin is allowed to use at runtime. */
    declaredCapabilities: Capability[];
    /** Allowed URL patterns for `platform.network.fetch`. */
    declaredEndpoints: string[];
    /** Host dismissal behavior for notifications created by this plugin. */
    dismissBehavior: DismissBehavior;
    /** Minimum compatible native bridge version. */
    minPlatformVersion: string;
    /**
     * Render mode. `'script'` (default) loads the JS bundle in a WebView.
     * `'template'` ships no JS and uses a native Compose card driven by
     * [template]. Server defaults to `'script'` when omitted.
     */
    renderer?: 'script' | 'template';
    /**
     * Template manifest. Required when [renderer] is `'template'`; rejected
     * when [renderer] is `'script'`. Validated server-side at publish time.
     */
    template?: TemplateBlock;
    /**
     * Card delivery semantics. `'event'` (default) ג€” each send is a new
     * immutable inbox row. `'live'` ג€” persistent, upsertable; see
     * `docs/integration-guide.md ֲ§5.2`. Server defaults to `'event'`.
     */
    cardType?: 'event' | 'live';
    /**
     * JSONPath into the decrypted payload that yields the stable card
     * identity. REQUIRED when [cardType] is `'live'`; rejected otherwise.
     * V1 validates only `startsWith("$")` server-side.
     */
    cardKeyPath?: string;
}
/**
 * Error raised when plugin manifest validation fails.
 */
export declare class ManifestValidationError extends Error {
    /** Individual validation failures. */
    readonly issues: string[];
    constructor(issues: string[]);
